      ### 🔍 How to Find More Detailed Numbers
      
      To get deeper into this data, here are some practical next steps:
      
      *   **Go Directly to Organizations**: For the most accurate numbers, reach out to the specific organization's development or communications department. They are often the best source for their own historical data.
      *   **Check County and School Reports**:
          *   The **County of Orange Social Services Agency (SSA)** publishes annual reports (like for FY 2024-2025) that can provide county-level context[reference:13].
          *   The **Annual Report on the Conditions of Children in Orange County** is another key county-level resource[reference:14].
          *   School data, often collected under the federal **McKinney-Vento Homeless Assistance Act**, can provide a more accurate picture of youth homelessness than shelter counts[reference:15].

      The plan involves four rounds of parallel searches to gather contact details (addresses, phones, emails, websites) and medical director/physician information for each organization.
      
      The first round of searches is designed to capture general contact pages, "Contact Us" pages, and medical staff directories for all organizations simultaneously. This approach will help build a foundation of data to review and refine in subsequent rounds.The search results for the first batch of organizations have provided some contact details.
